        list of solar eclipses in the 14th century BC
       </b>
       . During the period 1400 to 1301 BC there were 234 solar eclipses of which 76 were partial, 84 were annular (one
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Terminology" title="Solar eclipse">
        non-central
       </a>
       ), 68 were total, and 6 were hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year was four, occurring in 6 different years: 1372 BC, 1354 BC, 1336 BC, 1332 BC, 1318 BC, and 1307 BC.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div style="clear:both;">
      </div>
